<script type="text/javascript">(function(){var UP='up',DOWN='down',PX='px',RETRACT_NAV='chrome-v5-retract-nav-enabled',SLIDE='slide-up',maxSteps=10,duration=200,slideZIndex=1,navbar=document.getElementById('responsive-nav-scrollable'),header=document.getElementById('header'),topHeader=document.getElementById('top-header'),searchbox=document.getElementById('main-search-box'),isApollo1=header.className.indexOf('apollo-1')>0,topHeaderHeight=topHeader.offsetHeight,originalHeight=navbar.offsetHeight,originalZ=navbar.style.zIndex,direction=null,doAnimate=false,visibleNavOnTop=true,lastY=window.pageYOffset,interval=Math.floor(duration/maxSteps),animating=false,preventOpenTillUp=false,hasOwnProperty=Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty,distance=0,threshold=60,mouseMoveCount=0,makeLiHomepage=document.getElementById('make-linkedin-homepage'),homepageURL="https:\/\/www.linkedin.com\/",responsiveClassNames=['globalnav-show','globalnav-hide','globalnav-showStart','globalnav-hideStart','globalnav-showStop','globalnav-hideStop'],defaults,getOffset,originalOffset,addEvent,removeEvent,hasClass,addClass,removeClass,addResponsiveClass,removeResponsiveClasses,fireEvent,contains,mouseEnterLeave,animate,mouseOpen,mouseClose,mouseOpenTimer,mouseCloseTimer,staticPositionNav,fixedPositionNav;lastY=lastY||document.body.scrollTop;lastY=lastY||Math.max(document.documentElement.scrollTop,lastY);defaults=function(dest,defs){for(var prop in defs){if(!hasOwnProperty.call(dest,prop)){dest[prop]=defs[prop];}}
return dest;};getOffset=function(el){var _x=0,_y=0;while(el&&!isNaN(el.offsetLeft)&&!isNaN(el.offsetTop)){_x+=el.offsetLeft-el.scrollLeft;_y+=el.offsetTop-el.scrollTop;el=el.offsetParent;}
return{top:_y,left:_x};};originalOffset=getOffset(navbar);addEvent=(function(){if(window.addEventListener){return function(el,ev,fn){el.addEventListener(ev,fn,false);};}
else if(window.attachEvent){return function(el,ev,fn){el.attachEvent('on'+ev,fn);};}
else{return function(el,ev,fn){var oldFn=el['on'+ev]||function(){};el['on'+ev]=function(){oldFn();fn();};};}})();removeEvent=(function(){if(window.removeEventListener){return function(el,ev,fn){el.removeEventListener(ev,fn,false);}}else if(window.detachEvent){return function(el,ev,fn){el.detachEvent('on'+ev,fn);}}else{return function(el,ev,fn){el['on'+ev]=null;}}})();addResponsiveClass=function(responsiveClass){if(responsiveClassNames.indexOf(responsiveClass)!==-1){removeResponsiveClasses();addClass(document.getElementById('body'),responsiveClass);}};removeResponsiveClasses=function(){var i=0,responsiveClassName=responsiveClassNames[i],bodyEl=document.getElementById('body');while(responsiveClassName){removeClass(bodyEl,responsiveClassName);responsiveClassName=responsiveClassNames[++i];}};fireEvent=function(type,opts){var triggerFn,eventName='globalnav:'+type,className='globalnav-'+type;opts=opts||{};if(LI.Events){triggerFn=LI.Events.trigger||LI.Events.fire;if(typeof triggerFn==='function'){triggerFn.call(LI.Events,eventName,defaults(opts,{name:eventName}));}}
if(hasClass(document.body,RETRACT_NAV)){addResponsiveClass(className);}};mouseEnterLeave=function(element,type,callback){var preCallback,mouseEnter=type==='mouseenter',type=mouseEnter?'mouseover':'mouseout',ie=mouseEnter?'fromElement':'toElement';preCallback=function(event){event=event||window.event;var target=event.target||event.srcElement,related=event.relatedTarget||event[ie];if((element===target||contains(element,target))&&!contains(element,related)){callback();}};addEvent(element,type,preCallback);return preCallback;}
contains=function(container,element){return container.contains?container.contains(element):!!(container.compareDocumentPosition(element)&16);}
hasClass=function(el,test){var rHasClass=new RegExp('(?:^|\\s+)'+test+'(?:\\s+|$)');if(el&&el.nodeType===1&&rHasClass.test(el.className)){return true;}
return false;};addClass=function(el,newClass){if(el&&el.nodeType===1&&typeof newClass==='string'&&!hasClass(el,newClass)){el.className=el.className+' '+newClass;}};removeClass=function(el,killClass){if(el&&el.nodeType===1&&typeof killClass==='string'&&hasClass(el,killClass)){el.className=el.className.replace(new RegExp('(?:^|\\s+)'+killClass+'(?:\\s+|$)'),' ');}};animate=function(opts){var start=new Date(),id;if(opts.onStart){opts.onStart();}
id=setInterval(function(){var timePassed=new Date()-start,progress=timePassed/opts.duration,delta;if(progress>1){progress=1;}
delta=opts.delta(progress);opts.step(delta);if(progress===1){clearInterval(id);if(opts.onComplete){opts.onComplete();}}},opts.delay||10);return id;};staticPositionNav=function(){navbar.style.position='static';navbar.style.zIndex=originalZ;navbar.style.width='auto';navbar.style.top=null;};fixedPositionNav=function(){navbar.style.position='fixed';navbar.style.zIndex=slideZIndex;navbar.style.width=navbar.parentNode.clientWidth+PX;};if(makeLiHomepage){addEvent(makeLiHomepage,"click",function(evt){var e=evt||window.event;if(window.ActiveXObject&&homepageURL){document.body.style.behavior='url(#default#homepage)';document.body.setHomePage(homepageURL);}
if(e.preventDefault){e.preventDefault();}else{e.returnValue=false;}
return false;});}
addEvent(searchbox,'focus',function(){if(isApollo1){removeClass(header,SLIDE);}});addEvent(window,'scroll',function(){var currentY=window.pageYOffset;currentY=currentY||document.body.scrollTop;currentY=currentY||Math.max(document.documentElement.scrollTop,currentY);if(0>lastY){lastY=0;}
if(currentY>lastY&&direction!==DOWN){doAnimate=true;direction=DOWN;distance=0;if(preventOpenTillUp){doAnimate=false;}}
else if(lastY>currentY&&direction!==UP){distance+=(lastY-currentY);if(distance>threshold||currentY==0){doAnimate=true;direction=UP;preventOpenTillUp=false;distance=0;}}
else{distance=0;}
lastY=currentY;if(!doAnimate){return;}
doAnimate=false;if(animating){clearInterval(animating);}
animating=animate({delay:interval,duration:duration,delta:function(progress){return progress;},onStart:function(){fixedPositionNav();fireEvent(((direction===UP)?'show':'hide')+'Start');},step:function(delta){var heightDelta=(originalHeight*delta),newNavHeight,eventName;if(direction===DOWN){newNavHeight=originalHeight-heightDelta;navbar.style.top=(originalOffset.top-heightDelta-1)+PX;visibleNavOnTop=false;eventName='hide:animation:step';if(isApollo1){addClass(header,'slide-up');}}else{newNavHeight=heightDelta;navbar.style.top=((originalOffset.top-originalHeight)+heightDelta)+PX;eventName='show:animation:step';if(isApollo1){removeClass(header,'slide-up');}}
fireEvent(eventName,{delta:delta,headerHeight:newNavHeight+topHeaderHeight});},onComplete:function(){if(direction==UP){staticPositionNav();fireEvent('showStop');visibleNavOnTop=true;}else{fireEvent('hideStop');}}});});mouseOpen=function(){if(!visibleNavOnTop){staticPositionNav();fireEvent('show');}};mouseClose=function(){if(!visibleNavOnTop){fixedPositionNav();fireEvent('hide');navbar.style.top=originalOffset.top-originalHeight+PX;}};mouseEnterLeave(header,'mouseenter',function(){if(!preventOpenTillUp||mouseMoveCount>1){if(mouseOpenTimer){clearTimeout(mouseOpenTimer);}
if(mouseCloseTimer){clearTimeout(mouseCloseTimer);}
mouseOpenTimer=setTimeout(mouseOpen,100);}});mouseEnterLeave(header,'mouseleave',function(){if(mouseOpenTimer){clearTimeout(mouseOpenTimer);}
if(mouseCloseTimer){clearTimeout(mouseCloseTimer);}
mouseCloseTimer=setTimeout(mouseClose,300);});incrementMouseMove=function(){mouseMoveCount++;if(mouseMoveCount>1){removeEvent(document,'mousemove',incrementMouseMove);}};preventOpenTillUp=hasClass(document.body,RETRACT_NAV);if(preventOpenTillUp){addEvent(document,'mousemove',incrementMouseMove);}
if(preventOpenTillUp){fixedPositionNav();navbar.style.top=originalOffset.top-originalHeight+PX;visibleNavOnTop=false;}})();</script>
